<h2 id="examples" class="fs_1.5em mt_2em mb_1em lh_1.3333333 fw_700 c_var(--colors-prose-heading) [&amp;_strong]:fw_800 [&amp;_strong]:c_inherit [&amp;_code]:fs_0.875em [&amp;_+_*]:mt_0"><a class="link subheading-anchor" aria-label="Link to section" href="#examples"><span class="icon icon-link"></span></a>Examples</h2>
<div class="d_flex flex-d_column gap_0 not-prose [&amp;_&gt;_.example-preview-scope]:bdr-b_0"><div class="d_flex min-h_32 md:min-h_48 bg_bg.default bdr_lg bd-w_1px w_full ov_hidden not-prose example-preview-scope"><div class="d_flex flex-d_column ai_center jc_center flex_1 p_4 md:p_6 w_full"><div class="example-spinner" role="status" aria-label="Loading example"></div></div></div><div data-scope="collapsible" data-part="root" data-state="closed" dir="ltr" id="collapsible:_R_4bhanpfn5tlb_"><button class="button button--variant_outline button--size_xs bd-c_inherit c_fg.default w_full bdr-t_0 bd-t-w_0 bg_bg.default c_fg.muted fw_medium fs_xs gap_1.5 hover:bg_gray.2 hover:c_fg.default" data-scope="collapsible" data-part="trigger" id="collapsible:_R_4bhanpfn5tlb_:trigger" dir="ltr" type="button" data-state="closed" aria-controls="collapsible:_R_4bhanpfn5tlb_:content" aria-expanded="false"><svg xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" width="24" height="24" viewBox="0 0 24 24" fill="none" stroke="currentColor" stroke-width="2" stroke-linecap="round" stroke-linejoin="round" class="lucide lucide-code icon icon--size_sm" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m16 18 6-6-6-6"></path><path d="m8 6-6 6 6 6"></path></svg>Show Code</button></div></div>
<h3 id="controlled" class="fs_1.25em lh_1.6 mt_1.6em mb_0.6em fw_600 c_var(--colors-prose-heading) [&amp;_strong]:fw_700 [&amp;_strong]:c_inherit [&amp;_code]:fs_0.9em [&amp;_+_*]:mt_0"><a class="link subheading-anchor" aria-label="Link to section" href="#controlled"><span class="icon icon-link"></span></a>Controlled</h3>
<p class="mt_1.25em mb_1.25em c_var(--colors-prose-body) [&amp;_a]:td_underline [&amp;_a]:fw_500">Control the clipboard value externally by managing the state yourself and using <code class="c_var(--colors-prose-code) fw_600 bd-w_1px fs_0.875em p_0.125em_0.25em bdr_0.25em bg-c_gray.a2">onValueChange</code> to handle updates.</p>
<div class="d_flex flex-d_column gap_0 not-prose [&amp;_&gt;_.example-preview-scope]:bdr-b_0"><div class="d_flex min-h_32 md:min-h_48 bg_bg.default bdr_lg bd-w_1px w_full ov_hidden not-prose example-preview-scope"><div class="d_flex flex-d_column ai_center jc_center flex_1 p_4 md:p_6 w_full"><div class="example-spinner" role="status" aria-label="Loading example"></div></div></div><div data-scope="collapsible" data-part="root" data-state="closed" dir="ltr" id="collapsible:_R_4hhanpfn5tlb_"><button class="button button--variant_outline button--size_xs bd-c_inherit c_fg.default w_full bdr-t_0 bd-t-w_0 bg_bg.default c_fg.muted fw_medium fs_xs gap_1.5 hover:bg_gray.2 hover:c_fg.default" data-scope="collapsible" data-part="trigger" id="collapsible:_R_4hhanpfn5tlb_:trigger" dir="ltr" type="button" data-state="closed" aria-controls="collapsible:_R_4hhanpfn5tlb_:content" aria-expanded="false"><svg xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" width="24" height="24" viewBox="0 0 24 24" fill="none" stroke="currentColor" stroke-width="2" stroke-linecap="round" stroke-linejoin="round" class="lucide lucide-code icon icon--size_sm" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m16 18 6-6-6-6"></path><path d="m8 6-6 6 6 6"></path></svg>Show Code</button></div></div>
<h3 id="root-provider" class="fs_1.25em lh_1.6 mt_1.6em mb_0.6em fw_600 c_var(--colors-prose-heading) [&amp;_strong]:fw_700 [&amp;_strong]:c_inherit [&amp;_code]:fs_0.9em [&amp;_+_*]:mt_0"><a class="link subheading-anchor" aria-label="Link to section" href="#root-provider"><span class="icon icon-link"></span></a>Root Provider</h3>
<p class="mt_1.25em mb_1.25em c_var(--colors-prose-body) [&amp;_a]:td_underline [&amp;_a]:fw_500">An alternative way to control the clipboard is to use the <code class="c_var(--colors-prose-code) fw_600 bd-w_1px fs_0.875em p_0.125em_0.25em bdr_0.25em bg-c_gray.a2">RootProvider</code> component and the <code class="c_var(--colors-prose-code) fw_600 bd-w_1px fs_0.875em p_0.125em_0.25em bdr_0.25em bg-c_gray.a2">useClipboard</code> hook. This way
you can access the state and methods from outside the component.</p>
<div class="d_flex flex-d_column gap_0 not-prose [&amp;_&gt;_.example-preview-scope]:bdr-b_0"><div class="d_flex min-h_32 md:min-h_48 bg_bg.default bdr_lg bd-w_1px w_full ov_hidden not-prose example-preview-scope"><div class="d_flex flex-d_column ai_center jc_center flex_1 p_4 md:p_6 w_full"><div class="example-spinner" role="status" aria-label="Loading example"></div></div></div><div data-scope="collapsible" data-part="root" data-state="closed" dir="ltr" id="collapsible:_R_4nhanpfn5tlb_"><button class="button button--variant_outline button--size_xs bd-c_inherit c_fg.default w_full bdr-t_0 bd-t-w_0 bg_bg.default c_fg.muted fw_medium fs_xs gap_1.5 hover:bg_gray.2 hover:c_fg.default" data-scope="collapsible" data-part="trigger" id="collapsible:_R_4nhanpfn5tlb_:trigger" dir="ltr" type="button" data-state="closed" aria-controls="collapsible:_R_4nhanpfn5tlb_:content" aria-expanded="false"><svg xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" width="24" height="24" viewBox="0 0 24 24" fill="none" stroke="currentColor" stroke-width="2" stroke-linecap="round" stroke-linejoin="round" class="lucide lucide-code icon icon--size_sm" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m16 18 6-6-6-6"></path><path d="m8 6-6 6 6 6"></path></svg>Show Code</button></div></div>
<h3 id="context" class="fs_1.25em lh_1.6 mt_1.6em mb_0.6em fw_600 c_var(--colors-prose-heading) [&amp;_strong]:fw_700 [&amp;_strong]:c_inherit [&amp;_code]:fs_0.9em [&amp;_+_*]:mt_0"><a class="link subheading-anchor" aria-label="Link to section" href="#context"><span class="icon icon-link"></span></a>Context</h3>
<p class="mt_1.25em mb_1.25em c_var(--colors-prose-body) [&amp;_a]:td_underline [&amp;_a]:fw_500">Access the clipboard&#x27;s state with <code class="c_var(--colors-prose-code) fw_600 bd-w_1px fs_0.875em p_0.125em_0.25em bdr_0.25em bg-c_gray.a2">Clipboard.Context</code> or the <code class="c_var(--colors-prose-code) fw_600 bd-w_1px fs_0.875em p_0.125em_0.25em bdr_0.25em bg-c_gray.a2">useClipboardContext</code> hook. You get properties like
<code class="c_var(--colors-prose-code) fw_600 bd-w_1px fs_0.875em p_0.125em_0.25em bdr_0.25em bg-c_gray.a2">copied</code>, <code class="c_var(--colors-prose-code) fw_600 bd-w_1px fs_0.875em p_0.125em_0.25em bdr_0.25em bg-c_gray.a2">value</code>, and <code class="c_var(--colors-prose-code) fw_600 bd-w_1px fs_0.875em p_0.125em_0.25em bdr_0.25em bg-c_gray.a2">setValue</code>.</p>
<blockquote class="mt_1.6em mb_1.6em ps_1em fw_500 font-style_italic bd-s-w_0.25rem bd-c_var(--colors-prose-quote-border)">
<p class="mt_1.25em mb_1.25em c_var(--colors-prose-body) [&amp;_a]:td_underline [&amp;_a]:fw_500">Alternatively, you can use the <code class="c_var(--colors-prose-code) fw_600 bd-w_1px fs_0.875em p_0.125em_0.25em bdr_0.25em bg-c_gray.a2">useClipboardContext</code> hook to access the clipboard context.</p>
</blockquote>
<div class="d_flex flex-d_column gap_0 not-prose [&amp;_&gt;_.example-preview-scope]:bdr-b_0"><div class="d_flex min-h_32 md:min-h_48 bg_bg.default bdr_lg bd-w_1px w_full ov_hidden not-prose example-preview-scope"><div class="d_flex flex-d_column ai_center jc_center flex_1 p_4 md:p_6 w_full"><div class="example-spinner" role="status" aria-label="Loading example"></div></div></div><div data-scope="collapsible" data-part="root" data-state="closed" dir="ltr" id="collapsible:_R_4vhanpfn5tlb_"><button class="button button--variant_outline button--size_xs bd-c_inherit c_fg.default w_full bdr-t_0 bd-t-w_0 bg_bg.default c_fg.muted fw_medium fs_xs gap_1.5 hover:bg_gray.2 hover:c_fg.default" data-scope="collapsible" data-part="trigger" id="collapsible:_R_4vhanpfn5tlb_:trigger" dir="ltr" type="button" data-state="closed" aria-controls="collapsible:_R_4vhanpfn5tlb_:content" aria-expanded="false"><svg xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" width="24" height="24" viewBox="0 0 24 24" fill="none" stroke="currentColor" stroke-width="2" stroke-linecap="round" stroke-linejoin="round" class="lucide lucide-code icon icon--size_sm" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m16 18 6-6-6-6"></path><path d="m8 6-6 6 6 6"></path></svg>Show Code</button></div></div>
<h3 id="copy-status" class="fs_1.25em lh_1.6 mt_1.6em mb_0.6em fw_600 c_var(--colors-prose-heading) [&amp;_strong]:fw_700 [&amp;_strong]:c_inherit [&amp;_code]:fs_0.9em [&amp;_+_*]:mt_0"><a class="link subheading-anchor" aria-label="Link to section" href="#copy-status"><span class="icon icon-link"></span></a>Copy Status</h3>
<p class="mt_1.25em mb_1.25em c_var(--colors-prose-body) [&amp;_a]:td_underline [&amp;_a]:fw_500">Use the <code class="c_var(--colors-prose-code) fw_600 bd-w_1px fs_0.875em p_0.125em_0.25em bdr_0.25em bg-c_gray.a2">onStatusChange</code> prop to listen for copy operations. It exposes a <code class="c_var(--colors-prose-code) fw_600 bd-w_1px fs_0.875em p_0.125em_0.25em bdr_0.25em bg-c_gray.a2">copied</code> property that you can use to display
a success message.</p>
<div class="d_flex flex-d_column gap_0 not-prose [&amp;_&gt;_.example-preview-scope]:bdr-b_0"><div class="d_flex min-h_32 md:min-h_48 bg_bg.default bdr_lg bd-w_1px w_full ov_hidden not-prose example-preview-scope"><div class="d_flex flex-d_column ai_center jc_center flex_1 p_4 md:p_6 w_full"><div class="example-spinner" role="status" aria-label="Loading example"></div></div></div><div data-scope="collapsible" data-part="root" data-state="closed" dir="ltr" id="collapsible:_R_55hanpfn5tlb_"><button class="button button--variant_outline button--size_xs bd-c_inherit c_fg.default w_full bdr-t_0 bd-t-w_0 bg_bg.default c_fg.muted fw_medium fs_xs gap_1.5 hover:bg_gray.2 hover:c_fg.default" data-scope="collapsible" data-part="trigger" id="collapsible:_R_55hanpfn5tlb_:trigger" dir="ltr" type="button" data-state="closed" aria-controls="collapsible:_R_55hanpfn5tlb_:content" aria-expanded="false"><svg xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" width="24" height="24" viewBox="0 0 24 24" fill="none" stroke="currentColor" stroke-width="2" stroke-linecap="round" stroke-linejoin="round" class="lucide lucide-code icon icon--size_sm" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m16 18 6-6-6-6"></path><path d="m8 6-6 6 6 6"></path></svg>Show Code</button></div></div>
<h3 id="timeout" class="fs_1.25em lh_1.6 mt_1.6em mb_0.6em fw_600 c_var(--colors-prose-heading) [&amp;_strong]:fw_700 [&amp;_strong]:c_inherit [&amp;_code]:fs_0.9em [&amp;_+_*]:mt_0"><a class="link subheading-anchor" aria-label="Link to section" href="#timeout"><span class="icon icon-link"></span></a>Timeout</h3>
<p class="mt_1.25em mb_1.25em c_var(--colors-prose-body) [&amp;_a]:td_underline [&amp;_a]:fw_500">Configure the copy status timeout duration using the <code class="c_var(--colors-prose-code) fw_600 bd-w_1px fs_0.875em p_0.125em_0.25em bdr_0.25em bg-c_gray.a2">timeout</code> prop. Default is 3000ms (3 seconds).</p>
<div class="d_flex flex-d_column gap_0 not-prose [&amp;_&gt;_.example-preview-scope]:bdr-b_0"><div class="d_flex min-h_32 md:min-h_48 bg_bg.default bdr_lg bd-w_1px w_full ov_hidden not-prose example-preview-scope"><div class="d_flex flex-d_column ai_center jc_center flex_1 p_4 md:p_6 w_full"><div class="example-spinner" role="status" aria-label="Loading example"></div></div></div><div data-scope="collapsible" data-part="root" data-state="closed" dir="ltr" id="collapsible:_R_5bhanpfn5tlb_"><button class="button button--variant_outline button--size_xs bd-c_inherit c_fg.default w_full bdr-t_0 bd-t-w_0 bg_bg.default c_fg.muted fw_medium fs_xs gap_1.5 hover:bg_gray.2 hover:c_fg.default" data-scope="collapsible" data-part="trigger" id="collapsible:_R_5bhanpfn5tlb_:trigger" dir="ltr" type="button" data-state="closed" aria-controls="collapsible:_R_5bhanpfn5tlb_:content" aria-expanded="false"><svg xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" width="24" height="24" viewBox="0 0 24 24" fill="none" stroke="currentColor" stroke-width="2" stroke-linecap="round" stroke-linejoin="round" class="lucide lucide-code icon icon--size_sm" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m16 18 6-6-6-6"></path><path d="m8 6-6 6 6 6"></path></svg>Show Code</button></div></div>
<h3 id="value-text" class="fs_1.25em lh_1.6 mt_1.6em mb_0.6em fw_600 c_var(--colors-prose-heading) [&amp;_strong]:fw_700 [&amp;_strong]:c_inherit [&amp;_code]:fs_0.9em [&amp;_+_*]:mt_0"><a class="link subheading-anchor" aria-label="Link to section" href="#value-text"><span class="icon icon-link"></span></a>Value Text</h3>
<p class="mt_1.25em mb_1.25em c_var(--colors-prose-body) [&amp;_a]:td_underline [&amp;_a]:fw_500">Use <code class="c_var(--colors-prose-code) fw_600 bd-w_1px fs_0.875em p_0.125em_0.25em bdr_0.25em bg-c_gray.a2">Clipboard.ValueText</code> to display the current clipboard value.</p>
<div class="d_flex flex-d_column gap_0 not-prose [&amp;_&gt;_.example-preview-scope]:bdr-b_0"><div class="d_flex min-h_32 md:min-h_48 bg_bg.default bdr_lg bd-w_1px w_full ov_hidden not-prose example-preview-scope"><div class="d_flex flex-d_column ai_center jc_center flex_1 p_4 md:p_6 w_full"><div class="example-spinner" role="status" aria-label="Loading example"></div></div></div><div data-scope="collapsible" data-part="root" data-state="closed" dir="ltr" id="collapsible:_R_5hhanpfn5tlb_"><button class="button button--variant_outline button--size_xs bd-c_inherit c_fg.default w_full bdr-t_0 bd-t-w_0 bg_bg.default c_fg.muted fw_medium fs_xs gap_1.5 hover:bg_gray.2 hover:c_fg.default" data-scope="collapsible" data-part="trigger" id="collapsible:_R_5hhanpfn5tlb_:trigger" dir="ltr" type="button" data-state="closed" aria-controls="collapsible:_R_5hhanpfn5tlb_:content" aria-expanded="false"><svg xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" width="24" height="24" viewBox="0 0 24 24" fill="none" stroke="currentColor" stroke-width="2" stroke-linecap="round" stroke-linejoin="round" class="lucide lucide-code icon icon--size_sm" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m16 18 6-6-6-6"></path><path d="m8 6-6 6 6 6"></path></svg>Show Code</button></div></div>
<h2 id="api-reference" class="fs_1.5em mt_2em mb_1em lh_1.3333333 fw_700 c_var(--colors-prose-heading) [&amp;_strong]:fw_800 [&amp;_strong]:c_inherit [&amp;_code]:fs_0.875em [&amp;_+_*]:mt_0"><a class="link subheading-anchor" aria-label="Link to section" href="#api-reference"><span class="icon icon-link"></span></a>API Reference</h2>

Anatomy\n\n\u003cAnatomy id=\"clipboard\" /\u003e\n\n```tsx\n\u003cClipboard.Root\u003e\n  \u003cClipboard.Label /\u003e\n  \u003cClipboard.Control\u003e\n    \u003cClipboard.Input /\u003e\n    \u003cClipboard.Trigger\u003e\n      \u003cClipboard.Indicator /\u003e\n    \u003c/Clipboard.Trigger\u003e\n  \u003c/Clipboard.Control\u003e\n\u003c/Clipboard.Root\u003e\n```\n\n## Examples\n\n**Example: basic**\n\n#### React\n\n```tsx\nimport { Clipboard } from '@ark-ui/react/clipboard'\nimport { CheckIcon, ClipboardCopyIcon } from 'lucide-react'\nimport styles from 'styles/clipboard.module.css'\n\nexport const Basic = () =\u003e {\n  return (\n    \u003cClipboard.Root className={styles.Root} value=\"https://ark-ui.com\"\u003e\n      \u003cClipboard.Label className={styles.Label}\u003eCopy this link\u003c/Clipboard.Label\u003e\n      \u003cClipboard.Control className={styles.Control}\u003e\n        \u003cClipboard.Input className={styles.Input} /\u003e\n        \u003cClipboard.Trigger className={styles.Trigger}\u003e\n          \u003cClipboard.Indicator className={styles.Indicator} copied={\u003cCheckIcon /\u003e}\u003e\n            \u003cClipboardCopyIcon /\u003e\n          \u003c/Clipboard.Indicator\u003e\n        \u003c/Clipboard.Trigger\u003e\n      \u003c/Clipboard.Control\u003e\n    \u003c/Clipboard.Root\u003e\n  )\n}\n\n```\n\n#### Solid\n\n```tsx\nimport { Clipboard } from '@ark-ui/solid/clipboard'\nimport { CheckIcon, ClipboardCopyIcon } from 'lucide-solid'\nimport styles from 'styles/clipboard.module.css'\n\nexport const Basic = () =\u003e {\n  return (\n    \u003cClipboard.Root class={styles.Root} value=\"https://ark-ui.com\"\u003e\n      \u003cClipboard.Label class={styles.Label}\u003eCopy this link\u003c/Clipboard.Label\u003e\n      \u003cClipboard.Control class={styles.Control}\u003e\n        \u003cClipboard.Input class={styles.Input} /\u003e\n        \u003cClipboard.Trigger class={styles.Trigger}\u003e\n          \u003cClipboard.Indicator class={styles.Indicator} copied={\u003cCheckIcon /\u003e}\u003e\n            \u003cClipboardCopyIcon /\u003e\n          \u003c/Clipboard.Indicator\u003e\n        \u003c/Clipboard.Trigger\u003e\n      \u003c/Clipboard.Control\u003e\n    \u003c/Clipboard.Root\u003e\n  )\n}\n\n```\n\n#### Vue\n\n```vue\n\u003cscript setup lang=\"ts\"\u003e\nimport { Clipboard } from '@ark-ui/vue/clipboard'\nimport { CheckIcon, ClipboardCopyIcon } from 'lucide-vue-next'\nimport styles from 'styles/clipboard.module.css'\n\u003c/script\u003e\n\n\u003ctemplate\u003e\n  \u003cClipboard.Root :class=\"styles.Root\" default-value=\"https://ark-ui.com\"\u003e\n    \u003cClipboard.Label :class=\"styles.Label\"\u003eCopy this link\u003c/Clipboard.Label\u003e\n    \u003cClipboard.Control :class=\"styles.Control\"\u003e\n      \u003cClipboard.Input :class=\"styles.Input\" /\u003e\n      \u003cClipboard.Trigger :class=\"styles.Trigger\"\u003e\n        \u003cClipboard.Indicator :class=\"styles.Indicator\"\u003e\n          \u003cClipboardCopyIcon /\u003e\n          \u003ctemplate #copied\u003e\n            \u003cCheckIcon /\u003e\n          \u003c/template\u003e\n        \u003c/Clipboard.Indicator\u003e\n      \u003c/Clipboard.Trigger\u003e\n    \u003c/Clipboard.Control\u003e\n  \u003c/Clipboard.Root\u003e\n\u003c/template\u003e\n\n```\n\n#### Svelte\n\n```svelte\n\u003cscript lang=\"ts\"\u003e\n  import { Clipboard } from '@ark-ui/svelte/clipboard'\n  import { CheckIcon, ClipboardCopyIcon } from 'lucide-svelte'\n  import styles from 'styles/clipboard.module.css'\n\u003c/script\u003e\n\n\u003cClipboard.Root class={styles.Root} value=\"https://ark-ui.com\"\u003e\n  \u003cClipboard.Label class={styles.Label}\u003eCopy this link\u003c/Clipboard.Label\u003e\n  \u003cClipboard.Control class={styles.Control}\u003e\n    \u003cClipboard.Input class={styles.Input} /\u003e\n    \u003cClipboard.Trigger class={styles.Trigger}\u003e\n      \u003cClipboard.Indicator class={styles.Indicator}\u003e\n        {#snippet copied()}\n          \u003cCheckIcon /\u003e\n        {/snippet}\n        \u003cClipboardCopyIcon /\u003e\n      \u003c/Clipboard.Indicator\u003e\n    \u003c/Clipboard.Trigger\u003e\n  \u003c/Clipboard.Control\u003e\n\u003c/Clipboard.Root\u003e\n\n```\n\n### Controlled\n\nControl the clipboard value externally by managing the state yourself and using `onValueChange` to handle updates.\n\n**Example: controlled**\n\n#### React\n\n```tsx\nimport { Clipboard } from '@ark-ui/react/clipboard'\nimport { CheckIcon, ClipboardCopyIcon } from 'lucide-react'\nimport { useState } from 'react'\nimport button from 'styles/button.module.css'\nimport styles from 'styles/clipboard.module.css'\n\nexport const Controlled = () =\u003e {\n  const [url, setUrl] = useState('https://ark-ui.com')\n\n  return (\n    \u003cdiv className=\"stack\"\u003e\n      \u003cClipboard.Root className={styles.Root} value={url} onValueChange={(details) =\u003e setUrl(details.value)}\u003e\n        \u003cClipboard.Label className={styles.Label}\u003eCopy this link\u003c/Clipboard.Label\u003e\n        \u003cClipboard.Control className={styles.Control}\u003e\n          \u003cClipboard.Input className={styles.Input} /\u003e\n          \u003cClipboard.Trigger className={styles.Trigger}\u003e\n            \u003cClipboard.Indicator className={styles.Indicator} copied={\u003cCheckIcon /\u003e}\u003e\n              \u003cClipboardCopyIcon /\u003e\n            \u003c/Clipboard.Indicator\u003e\n          \u003c/Clipboard.Trigger\u003e\n        \u003c/Clipboard.Control\u003e\n      \u003c/Clipboard.Root\u003e\n\n      \u003cbutton className={button.Root} onClick={() =\u003e setUrl('https://chakra-ui.com')}\u003e\n        Change Url\n      \u003c/button\u003e\n    \u003c/div\u003e\n  )\n}\n\n```\n\n#### Solid\n\n```tsx\nimport { Clipboard } from '@ark-ui/solid/clipboard'\nimport { CheckIcon, ClipboardCopyIcon } from 'lucide-solid'\nimport { createSignal } from 'solid-js'\nimport button from 'styles/button.module.css'\nimport styles from 'styles/clipboard.module.css'\n\nexport const Controlled = () =\u003e {\n  const [url, setUrl] = createSignal('https://ark-ui.com')\n\n  return (\n    \u003cdiv class=\"stack\"\u003e\n      \u003cClipboard.Root class={styles.Root} value={url()} onValueChange={(details) =\u003e setUrl(details.value)}\u003e\n        \u003cClipboard.Label class={styles.Label}\u003eCopy this link\u003c/Clipboard.Label\u003e\n        \u003cClipboard.Control class={styles.Control}\u003e\n          \u003cClipboard.Input class={styles.Input} /\u003e\n          \u003cClipboard.Trigger class={styles.Trigger}\u003e\n            \u003cClipboard.Indicator class={styles.Indicator} copied={\u003cCheckIcon /\u003e}\u003e\n              \u003cClipboardCopyIcon /\u003e\n            \u003c/Clipboard.Indicator\u003e\n          \u003c/Clipboard.Trigger\u003e\n        \u003c/Clipboard.Control\u003e\n      \u003c/Clipboard.Root\u003e\n\n      \u003cbutton class={button.Root} onClick={() =\u003e setUrl('https://chakra-ui.com')}\u003e\n        Change Url\n      \u003c/button\u003e\n    \u003c/div\u003e\n  )\n}\n\n```\n\n#### Vue\n\n```vue\n\u003cscript setup lang=\"ts\"\u003e\nimport { Clipboard } from '@ark-ui/vue/clipboard'\nimport { CheckIcon, ClipboardCopyIcon } from 'lucide-vue-next'\nimport { ref } from 'vue'\nimport button from 'styles/button.module.css'\nimport styles from 'styles/clipboard.module.css'\n\nconst url = ref('https://ark-ui.com')\n\u003c/script\u003e\n\n\u003ctemplate\u003e\n  \u003cdiv class=\"stack\"\u003e\n    \u003cClipboard.Root :class=\"styles.Root\" v-model=\"url\"\u003e\n      \u003cClipboard.Label :class=\"styles.Label\"\u003eCopy this link\u003c/Clipboard.Label\u003e\n      \u003cClipboard.Control :class=\"styles.Control\"\u003e\n        \u003cClipboard.Input :class=\"styles.Input\" /\u003e\n        \u003cClipboard.Trigger :class=\"styles.Trigger\"\u003e\n          \u003cClipboard.Indicator :class=\"styles.Indicator\"\u003e\n            \u003cClipboardCopyIcon /\u003e\n            \u003ctemplate #copied\u003e\n              \u003cCheckIcon /\u003e\n            \u003c/template\u003e\n          \u003c/Clipboard.Indicator\u003e\n        \u003c/Clipboard.Trigger\u003e\n      \u003c/Clipboard.Control\u003e\n    \u003c/Clipboard.Root\u003e\n\n    \u003cbutton :class=\"button.Root\" @click=\"url = 'https://chakra-ui.com'\"\u003eChange Url\u003c/button\u003e\n  \u003c/div\u003e\n\u003c/template\u003e\n\n```\n\n#### Svelte\n\n```svelte\n\u003cscript lang=\"ts\"\u003e\n  import { Clipboard } from '@ark-ui/svelte/clipboard'\n  import { CheckIcon, ClipboardCopyIcon } from 'lucide-svelte'\n  import button from 'styles/button.module.css'\n  import styles from 'styles/clipboard.module.css'\n\n  let url = $state('https://ark-ui.com')\n\u003c/script\u003e\n\n\u003cdiv class=\"stack\"\u003e\n  \u003cClipboard.Root class={styles.Root} bind:value={url}\u003e\n    \u003cClipboard.Label class={styles.Label}\u003eCopy this link\u003c/Clipboard.Label\u003e\n    \u003cClipboard.Control class={styles.Control}\u003e\n      \u003cClipboard.Input class={styles.Input} /\u003e\n      \u003cClipboard.Trigger class={styles.Trigger}\u003e\n        \u003cClipboard.Indicator class={styles.Indicator}\u003e\n          {#snippet copied()}\n            \u003cCheckIcon /\u003e\n          {/snippet}\n          \u003cClipboardCopyIcon /\u003e\n        \u003c/Clipboard.Indicator\u003e\n      \u003c/Clipboard.Trigger\u003e\n    \u003c/Clipboard.Control\u003e\n  \u003c/Clipboard.Root\u003e\n\n  \u003cbutton class={button.Root} onclick={() =\u003e (url = 'https://chakra-ui.com')}\u003eChange Url\u003c/button\u003e\n\u003c/div\u003e\n\n```\n\n### Root Provider\n\nAn alternative way to control the clipboard is to use the `RootProvider` component and the `useClipboard` hook. This way\nyou can access the state and methods from outside the component.\n\n**Example: root-provider**\n\n#### React\n\n```tsx\nimport { Clipboard, useClipboard } from '@ark-ui/react/clipboard'\nimport { CheckIcon, ClipboardCopyIcon } from 'lucide-react'\nimport styles from 'styles/clipboard.module.css'\n\nexport const RootProvider = () =\u003e {\n  const clipboard = useClipboard({ value: 'https://ark-ui.com' })\n\n  return (\n    \u003cdiv className=\"stack\"\u003e\n      \u003coutput\u003e\n        value: {clipboard.value}, copied: {String(clipboard.copied)}\n      \u003c/output\u003e\n      \u003cClipboard.RootProvider className={styles.Root} value={clipboard}\u003e\n        \u003cClipboard.Label className={styles.Label}\u003eCopy this link\u003c/Clipboard.Label\u003e\n        \u003cClipboard.Control className={styles.Control}\u003e\n          \u003cClipboard.Input className={styles.Input} /\u003e\n          \u003cClipboard.Trigger className={styles.Trigger}\u003e\n            \u003cClipboard.Indicator className={styles.Indicator} copied={\u003cCheckIcon /\u003e}\u003e\n              \u003cClipboardCopyIcon /\u003e\n            \u003c/Clipboard.Indicator\u003e\n          \u003c/Clipboard.Trigger\u003e\n        \u003c/Clipboard.Control\u003e\n      \u003c/Clipboard.RootProvider\u003e\n    \u003c/div\u003e\n  )\n}\n\n```\n\n#### Solid\n\n```tsx\nimport { Clipboard, useClipboard } from '@ark-ui/solid/clipboard'\nimport { CheckIcon, ClipboardCopyIcon } from 'lucide-solid'\nimport styles from 'styles/clipboard.module.css'\n\nexport const RootProvider = () =\u003e {\n  const clipboard = useClipboard({ value: 'https://ark-ui.com' })\n\n  return (\n    \u003cdiv class=\"stack\"\u003e\n      \u003coutput\u003e\n        value: {clipboard().value}, copied: {String(clipboard().copied)}\n      \u003c/output\u003e\n      \u003cClipboard.RootProvider class={styles.Root} value={clipboard}\u003e\n        \u003cClipboard.Label class={styles.Label}\u003eCopy this link\u003c/Clipboard.Label\u003e\n        \u003cClipboard.Control class={styles.Control}\u003e\n          \u003cClipboard.Input class={styles.Input} /\u003e\n          \u003cClipboard.Trigger class={styles.Trigger}\u003e\n            \u003cClipboard.Indicator class={styles.Indicator} copied={\u003cCheckIcon /\u003e}\u003e\n              \u003cClipboardCopyIcon /\u003e\n            \u003c/Clipboard.Indicator\u003e\n          \u003c/Clipboard.Trigger\u003e\n        \u003c/Clipboard.Control\u003e\n      \u003c/Clipboard.RootProvider\u003e\n    \u003c/div\u003e\n  )\n}\n\n```\n\n#### Vue\n\n```vue\n\u003cscript setup lang=\"ts\"\u003e\nimport { Clipboard, useClipboard } from '@ark-ui/vue/clipboard'\nimport { CheckIcon, ClipboardCopyIcon } from 'lucide-vue-next'\nimport styles from 'styles/clipboard.module.css'\n\nconst clipboard = useClipboard({ value: 'https://ark-ui.com' })\n\u003c/script\u003e\n\n\u003ctemplate\u003e\n  \u003cdiv class=\"stack\"\u003e\n    \u003coutput\u003evalue: {{ clipboard.value }}, copied: {{ String(clipboard.copied) }}\u003c/output\u003e\n    \u003cClipboard.RootProvider :class=\"styles.Root\" :value=\"clipboard\"\u003e\n      \u003cClipboard.Label :class=\"styles.Label\"\u003eCopy this link\u003c/Clipboard.Label\u003e\n      \u003cClipboard.Control :class=\"styles.Control\"\u003e\n        \u003cClipboard.Input :class=\"styles.Input\" /\u003e\n        \u003cClipboard.Trigger :class=\"styles.Trigger\"\u003e\n          \u003cClipboard.Indicator :class=\"styles.Indicator\"\u003e\n            \u003cClipboardCopyIcon /\u003e\n            \u003ctemplate #copied\u003e\n              \u003cCheckIcon /\u003e\n            \u003c/template\u003e\n          \u003c/Clipboard.Indicator\u003e\n        \u003c/Clipboard.Trigger\u003e\n      \u003c/Clipboard.Control\u003e\n    \u003c/Clipboard.RootProvider\u003e\n  \u003c/div\u003e\n\u003c/template\u003e\n\n```\n\n#### Svelte\n\n```svelte\n\u003cscript lang=\"ts\"\u003e\n  import { Clipboard, useClipboard } from '@ark-ui/svelte/clipboard'\n  import { CheckIcon, ClipboardCopyIcon } from 'lucide-svelte'\n  import styles from 'styles/clipboard.module.css'\n\n  const clipboard = useClipboard(() =\u003e ({ value: 'https://ark-ui.com' }))\n\u003c/script\u003e\n\n\u003cdiv class=\"stack\"\u003e\n  \u003coutput\u003e\n    value: {clipboard().value}, copied: {String(clipboard().copied)}\n  \u003c/output\u003e\n  \u003cClipboard.RootProvider class={styles.Root} value={clipboard}\u003e\n    \u003cClipboard.Label class={styles.Label}\u003eCopy this link\u003c/Clipboard.Label\u003e\n    \u003cClipboard.Control class={styles.Control}\u003e\n      \u003cClipboard.Input class={styles.Input} /\u003e\n      \u003cClipboard.Trigger class={styles.Trigger}\u003e\n        \u003cClipboard.Indicator class={styles.Indicator}\u003e\n          {#snippet copied()}\n            \u003cCheckIcon /\u003e\n          {/snippet}\n          \u003cClipboardCopyIcon /\u003e\n        \u003c/Clipboard.Indicator\u003e\n      \u003c/Clipboard.Trigger\u003e\n    \u003c/Clipboard.Control\u003e\n  \u003c/Clipboard.RootProvider\u003e\n\u003c/div\u003e\n\n```\n\n### Context\n\nAccess the clipboard's state with `Clipboard.Context` or the `useClipboardContext` hook. You get properties like\n`copied`, `value`, and `setValue`.\n\n\u003e Alternatively, you can use the `useClipboardContext` hook to access the clipboard context.\n\n**Example: context**\n\n#### React\n\n```tsx\nimport { Clipboard } from '@ark-ui/react/clipboard'\nimport { CheckIcon, ClipboardCopyIcon } from 'lucide-react'\nimport button from 'styles/button.module.css'\nimport styles from 'styles/clipboard.module.css'\n\nexport const Context = () =\u003e {\n  return (\n    \u003cClipboard.Root className={styles.Root} value=\"https://ark-ui.com\"\u003e\n      \u003cClipboard.Label className={styles.Label}\u003eCopy this link\u003c/Clipboard.Label\u003e\n      \u003cClipboard.Context\u003e\n        {(clipboard) =\u003e (\n          \u003cbutton className={button.Root} onClick={() =\u003e clipboard.copy()}\u003e\n            {clipboard.copied ? \u003cCheckIcon /\u003e : \u003cClipboardCopyIcon /\u003e}\n            {clipboard.copied ? 'Copied!' : 'Copy'}\n          \u003c/button\u003e\n        )}\n      \u003c/Clipboard.Context\u003e\n    \u003c/Clipboard.Root\u003e\n  )\n}\n\n```\n\n#### Solid\n\n```tsx\nimport { Clipboard } from '@ark-ui/solid/clipboard'\nimport { CheckIcon, ClipboardCopyIcon } from 'lucide-solid'\nimport { Show } from 'solid-js'\nimport button from 'styles/button.module.css'\nimport styles from 'styles/clipboard.module.css'\n\nexport const Context = () =\u003e {\n  return (\n    \u003cClipboard.Root class={styles.Root} value=\"https://ark-ui.com\"\u003e\n      \u003cClipboard.Label class={styles.Label}\u003eCopy this link\u003c/Clipboard.Label\u003e\n      \u003cClipboard.Context\u003e\n        {(clipboard) =\u003e (\n          \u003cbutton class={button.Root} onClick={() =\u003e clipboard().copy()}\u003e\n            \u003cShow when={clipboard().copied} fallback={\u003cClipboardCopyIcon /\u003e}\u003e\n              \u003cCheckIcon /\u003e\n            \u003c/Show\u003e\n            \u003cShow when={clipboard().copied} fallback=\"Copy\"\u003e\n              Copied!\n            \u003c/Show\u003e\n          \u003c/button\u003e\n        )}\n      \u003c/Clipboard.Context\u003e\n    \u003c/Clipboard.Root\u003e\n  )\n}\n\n```\n\n#### Vue\n\n```vue\n\u003cscript setup lang=\"ts\"\u003e\nimport { Clipboard } from '@ark-ui/vue/clipboard'\nimport { CheckIcon, ClipboardCopyIcon } from 'lucide-vue-next'\nimport button from 'styles/button.module.css'\nimport styles from 'styles/clipboard.module.css'\n\u003c/script\u003e\n\n\u003ctemplate\u003e\n  \u003cClipboard.Root :class=\"styles.Root\" default-value=\"https://ark-ui.com\"\u003e\n    \u003cClipboard.Label :class=\"styles.Label\"\u003eCopy this link\u003c/Clipboard.Label\u003e\n    \u003cClipboard.Context v-slot=\"clipboard\"\u003e\n      \u003cbutton :class=\"button.Root\" @click=\"clipboard.copy()\"\u003e\n        \u003cCheckIcon v-if=\"clipboard.copied\" /\u003e\n        \u003cClipboardCopyIcon v-else /\u003e\n        {{ clipboard.copied ? 'Copied!' : 'Copy' }}\n      \u003c/button\u003e\n    \u003c/Clipboard.Context\u003e\n  \u003c/Clipboard.Root\u003e\n\u003c/template\u003e\n\n```\n\n#### Svelte\n\n```svelte\n\u003cscript lang=\"ts\"\u003e\n  import { Clipboard } from '@ark-ui/svelte/clipboard'\n  import { CheckIcon, ClipboardCopyIcon } from 'lucide-svelte'\n  import button from 'styles/button.module.css'\n  import styles from 'styles/clipboard.module.css'\n\u003c/script\u003e\n\n\u003cClipboard.Root class={styles.Root} value=\"https://ark-ui.com\"\u003e\n  \u003cClipboard.Label class={styles.Label}\u003eCopy this link\u003c/Clipboard.Label\u003e\n  \u003cClipboard.Context\u003e\n    {#snippet render(clipboard)}\n      \u003cbutton class={button.Root} onclick={() =\u003e clipboard().copy()}\u003e\n        {#if clipboard().copied}\n          \u003cCheckIcon /\u003e\n          Copied!\n        {:else}\n          \u003cClipboardCopyIcon /\u003e\n          Copy\n        {/if}\n      \u003c/button\u003e\n    {/snippet}\n  \u003c/Clipboard.Context\u003e\n\u003c/Clipboard.Root\u003e\n\n```\n\n### Copy Status\n\nUse the `onStatusChange` prop to listen for copy operations. It exposes a `copied` property that you can use to display\na success message.\n\n**Example: copy-status**\n\n#### React\n\n```tsx\nimport { Clipboard } from '@ark-ui/react/clipboard'\nimport { CheckIcon, ClipboardCopyIcon } from 'lucide-react'\nimport { useState } from 'react'\nimport styles from 'styles/clipboard.module.css'\n\nexport const CopyStatus = () =\u003e {\n  const [copyCount, setCopyCount] = useState(0)\n\n  return (\n    \u003cClipboard.Root\n      className={styles.Root}\n      value=\"https://ark-ui.com\"\n      onStatusChange={(details) =\u003e {\n        if (details.copied) setCopyCount((prev) =\u003e prev + 1)\n      }}\n    \u003e\n      \u003cClipboard.Control className={styles.Control}\u003e\n        \u003cClipboard.Trigger className={styles.Trigger}\u003e\n          \u003cClipboard.Indicator className={styles.Indicator} copied={\u003cCheckIcon /\u003e}\u003e\n            \u003cClipboardCopyIcon /\u003e\n          \u003c/Clipboard.Indicator\u003e\n          \u003cClipboard.ValueText /\u003e\n        \u003c/Clipboard.Trigger\u003e\n      \u003c/Clipboard.Control\u003e\n      \u003cp\u003eCopied {copyCount} times\u003c/p\u003e\n    \u003c/Clipboard.Root\u003e\n  )\n}\n\n```\n\n#### Solid\n\n```tsx\nimport { Clipboard } from '@ark-ui/solid/clipboard'\nimport { CheckIcon, ClipboardCopyIcon } from 'lucide-solid'\nimport { createSignal } from 'solid-js'\nimport styles from 'styles/clipboard.module.css'\n\nexport const CopyStatus = () =\u003e {\n  const [copyCount, setCopyCount] = createSignal(0)\n\n  return (\n    \u003cClipboard.Root\n      class={styles.Root}\n      value=\"https://ark-ui.com\"\n      onStatusChange={(details) =\u003e {\n        if (details.copied) {\n          setCopyCount((prev) =\u003e prev + 1)\n        }\n      }}\n    \u003e\n      \u003cClipboard.Control class={styles.Control}\u003e\n        \u003cClipboard.Trigger class={styles.Trigger}\u003e\n          \u003cClipboard.Indicator class={styles.Indicator} copied={\u003cCheckIcon /\u003e}\u003e\n            \u003cClipboardCopyIcon /\u003e\n          \u003c/Clipboard.Indicator\u003e\n        \u003c/Clipboard.Trigger\u003e\n      \u003c/Clipboard.Control\u003e\n      \u003cp\u003eCopied {copyCount()} times\u003c/p\u003e\n    \u003c/Clipboard.Root\u003e\n  )\n}\n\n```\n\n#### Vue\n\n```vue\n\u003cscript setup lang=\"ts\"\u003e\nimport { Clipboard } from '@ark-ui/vue/clipboard'\nimport { CheckIcon, ClipboardCopyIcon } from 'lucide-vue-next'\nimport { ref } from 'vue'\nimport styles from 'styles/clipboard.module.css'\n\nconst copyCount = ref(0)\n\u003c/script\u003e\n\n\u003ctemplate\u003e\n  \u003cClipboard.Root\n    :class=\"styles.Root\"\n    default-value=\"https://ark-ui.com\"\n    @status-change=\"\n      (details) =\u003e {\n        if (details.copied) {\n          copyCount += 1\n        }\n      }\n    \"\n  \u003e\n    \u003cClipboard.Control :class=\"styles.Control\"\u003e\n      \u003cClipboard.Trigger :class=\"styles.Trigger\"\u003e\n        \u003cClipboard.Indicator :class=\"styles.Indicator\"\u003e\n          \u003cClipboardCopyIcon /\u003e\n          \u003ctemplate #copied\u003e\n            \u003cCheckIcon /\u003e\n          \u003c/template\u003e\n        \u003c/Clipboard.Indicator\u003e\n      \u003c/Clipboard.Trigger\u003e\n    \u003c/Clipboard.Control\u003e\n    \u003cp\u003eCopied {{ copyCount }} times\u003c/p\u003e\n  \u003c/Clipboard.Root\u003e\n\u003c/template\u003e\n\n```\n\n#### Svelte\n\n```svelte\n\u003cscript lang=\"ts\"\u003e\n  import { Clipboard } from '@ark-ui/svelte/clipboard'\n  import { CheckIcon, ClipboardCopyIcon } from 'lucide-svelte'\n  import styles from 'styles/clipboard.module.css'\n\n  let copyCount = $state(0)\n\u003c/script\u003e\n\n\u003cClipboard.Root\n  class={styles.Root}\n  value=\"https://ark-ui.com\"\n  onStatusChange={(details) =\u003e {\n    if (details.copied) {\n      copyCount += 1\n    }\n  }}\n\u003e\n  \u003cClipboard.Control class={styles.Control}\u003e\n    \u003cClipboard.Trigger class={styles.Trigger}\u003e\n      \u003cClipboard.Indicator class={styles.Indicator}\u003e\n        {#snippet copied()}\n          \u003cCheckIcon /\u003e\n        {/snippet}\n        \u003cClipboardCopyIcon /\u003e\n      \u003c/Clipboard.Indicator\u003e\n    \u003c/Clipboard.Trigger\u003e\n  \u003c/Clipboard.Control\u003e\n  \u003cp\u003eCopied {copyCount} times\u003c/p\u003e\n\u003c/Clipboard.Root\u003e\n\n```\n\n### Timeout\n\nConfigure the copy status timeout duration using the `timeout` prop. Default is 3000ms (3 seconds).\n\n**Example: timeout**\n\n#### React\n\n```tsx\nimport { Clipboard } from '@ark-ui/react/clipboard'\nimport { CheckIcon, ClipboardCopyIcon } from 'lucide-react'\nimport styles from 'styles/clipboard.module.css'\n\nexport const Timeout = () =\u003e {\n  return (\n    \u003cClipboard.Root className={styles.Root} value=\"https://ark-ui.com\" timeout={5000}\u003e\n      \u003cClipboard.Label className={styles.Label}\u003eCopy this link (5 second timeout)\u003c/Clipboard.Label\u003e\n      \u003cClipboard.Control className={styles.Control}\u003e\n        \u003cClipboard.Input className={styles.Input} /\u003e\n        \u003cClipboard.Trigger className={styles.Trigger}\u003e\n          \u003cClipboard.Indicator className={styles.Indicator} copied={\u003cCheckIcon /\u003e}\u003e\n            \u003cClipboardCopyIcon /\u003e\n          \u003c/Clipboard.Indicator\u003e\n        \u003c/Clipboard.Trigger\u003e\n      \u003c/Clipboard.Control\u003e\n    \u003c/Clipboard.Root\u003e\n  )\n}\n\n```\n\n#### Solid\n\n```tsx\nimport { Clipboard } from '@ark-ui/solid/clipboard'\nimport { CheckIcon, ClipboardCopyIcon } from 'lucide-solid'\nimport styles from 'styles/clipboard.module.css'\n\nexport const Timeout = () =\u003e {\n  return (\n    \u003cClipboard.Root class={styles.Root} value=\"https://ark-ui.com\" timeout={5000}\u003e\n      \u003cClipboard.Label class={styles.Label}\u003eCopy this link (5 second timeout)\u003c/Clipboard.Label\u003e\n      \u003cClipboard.Control class={styles.Control}\u003e\n        \u003cClipboard.Input class={styles.Input} /\u003e\n        \u003cClipboard.Trigger class={styles.Trigger}\u003e\n          \u003cClipboard.Indicator class={styles.Indicator} copied={\u003cCheckIcon /\u003e}\u003e\n            \u003cClipboardCopyIcon /\u003e\n          \u003c/Clipboard.Indicator\u003e\n        \u003c/Clipboard.Trigger\u003e\n      \u003c/Clipboard.Control\u003e\n    \u003c/Clipboard.Root\u003e\n  )\n}\n\n```\n\n#### Vue\n\n```vue\n\u003cscript setup lang=\"ts\"\u003e\nimport { Clipboard } from '@ark-ui/vue/clipboard'\nimport { CheckIcon, ClipboardCopyIcon } from 'lucide-vue-next'\nimport styles from 'styles/clipboard.module.css'\n\u003c/script\u003e\n\n\u003ctemplate\u003e\n  \u003cClipboard.Root :class=\"styles.Root\" default-value=\"https://ark-ui.com\" :timeout=\"5000\"\u003e\n    \u003cClipboard.Label :class=\"styles.Label\"\u003eCopy this link (5 second timeout)\u003c/Clipboard.Label\u003e\n    \u003cClipboard.Control :class=\"styles.Control\"\u003e\n      \u003cClipboard.Input :class=\"styles.Input\" /\u003e\n      \u003cClipboard.Trigger :class=\"styles.Trigger\"\u003e\n        \u003cClipboard.Indicator :class=\"styles.Indicator\"\u003e\n          \u003cClipboardCopyIcon /\u003e\n          \u003ctemplate #copied\u003e\n            \u003cCheckIcon /\u003e\n          \u003c/template\u003e\n        \u003c/Clipboard.Indicator\u003e\n      \u003c/Clipboard.Trigger\u003e\n    \u003c/Clipboard.Control\u003e\n  \u003c/Clipboard.Root\u003e\n\u003c/template\u003e\n\n```\n\n#### Svelte\n\n```svelte\n\u003cscript lang=\"ts\"\u003e\n  import { Clipboard } from '@ark-ui/svelte/clipboard'\n  import { CheckIcon, ClipboardCopyIcon } from 'lucide-svelte'\n  import styles from 'styles/clipboard.module.css'\n\u003c/script\u003e\n\n\u003cClipboard.Root class={styles.Root} value=\"https://ark-ui.com\" \u003cClipboard.Input class={styles.Input} /\u003e\n    \u003cClipboard.Trigger class={styles.Trigger}\u003e\n      \u003cClipboard.Indicator class={styles.Indicator}\u003e\n        {#snippet copied()}\n          \u003cCheckIcon /\u003e\n        {/snippet}\n        \u003cClipboardCopyIcon /\u003e\n      \u003c/Clipboard.Indicator\u003e\n    \u003c/Clipboard.Trigger\u003e\n  \u003c/Clipboard.Control\u003e\n\u003c/Clipboard.Root\u003e\n\n```\n\n### Value Text\n\nUse `Clipboard.ValueText` to display the current clipboard value.\n\n**Example: value-text**\n\n#### React\n\n```tsx\nimport { Clipboard } from '@ark-ui/react/clipboard'\nimport { CheckIcon, ClipboardCopyIcon } from 'lucide-react'\nimport styles from 'styles/clipboard.module.css'\n\nexport const ValueText = () =\u003e {\n  return (\n    \u003cClipboard.Root className={styles.Root} value=\"https://ark-ui.com\"\u003e\n      \u003cClipboard.Control className={styles.Control}\u003e\n        \u003cClipboard.ValueText className={styles.ValueText} /\u003e\n        \u003cClipboard.Trigger className={styles.Trigger}\u003e\n          \u003cClipboard.Indicator className={styles.Indicator} copied={\u003cCheckIcon /\u003e}\u003e\n            \u003cClipboardCopyIcon /\u003e\n          \u003c/Clipboard.Indicator\u003e\n        \u003c/Clipboard.Trigger\u003e\n      \u003c/Clipboard.Control\u003e\n    \u003c/Clipboard.Root\u003e\n  )\n}\n\n```\n\n#### Solid\n\n```tsx\nimport { Clipboard } from '@ark-ui/solid/clipboard'\nimport { CheckIcon, ClipboardCopyIcon } from 'lucide-solid'\nimport styles from 'styles/clipboard.module.css'\n\nexport const ValueText = () =\u003e {\n  return (\n    \u003cClipboard.Root class={styles.Root} value=\"https://ark-ui.com\"\u003e\n      \u003cClipboard.Control class={styles.Control}\u003e\n        \u003cClipboard.ValueText class={styles.ValueText} /\u003e\n        \u003cClipboard.Trigger class={styles.Trigger}\u003e\n          \u003cClipboard.Indicator class={styles.Indicator} copied={\u003cCheckIcon /\u003e}\u003e\n            \u003cClipboardCopyIcon /\u003e\n          \u003c/Clipboard.Indicator\u003e\n        \u003c/Clipboard.Trigger\u003e\n      \u003c/Clipboard.Control\u003e\n    \u003c/Clipboard.Root\u003e\n  )\n}\n\n```\n\n#### Vue\n\n```vue\n\u003cscript setup lang=\"ts\"\u003e\nimport { Clipboard } from '@ark-ui/vue/clipboard'\nimport { CheckIcon, ClipboardCopyIcon } from 'lucide-vue-next'\nimport styles from 'styles/clipboard.module.css'\n\u003c/script\u003e\n\n\u003ctemplate\u003e\n  \u003cClipboard.Root :class=\"styles.Root\" default-value=\"https://ark-ui.com\"\u003e\n    \u003cClipboard.Control :class=\"styles.Control\"\u003e\n      \u003cClipboard.ValueText :class=\"styles.ValueText\" /\u003e\n      \u003cClipboard.Trigger :class=\"styles.Trigger\"\u003e\n        \u003cClipboard.Indicator :class=\"styles.Indicator\"\u003e\n          \u003cClipboardCopyIcon /\u003e\n          \u003ctemplate #copied\u003e\n            \u003cCheckIcon /\u003e\n          \u003c/template\u003e\n
